I don't have enough room to tell you how WONDERFUL Tamira restaurant is!!! We catered a holiday party at our home for 40 people. Not only was Remmie the owner INCREDIBLE to work with, but the food was OUTSTANDING!!! What a treat for all our guests. It was very reasonably priced, and HUGE portions. I would order again and again for all my parties, and our guests raved all night about how delicious the food was. We had so many selections. I often eat my main meal of the day at lunch time between 12-2 p.m. I look for Fresh food from Salads to Meats. So Tamira is one of my favorite places to enjoy my lunch. <Pictures>None< /Pictures><text>Came for a late lunch buffet. The staff was pretty kind and the place was very clean. There wasn't a wide range of options in the buffet, however the food quality was over the average (neither too salty nor too spicy at all). Tried the tandoori chicken, which was perfectly marinated and grilled (maybe a little bit dry). I also tried some of the vegetable options, which were good, especially the aloo zucchini and potato. The chicken tikka masala was OK. There were some other fresh salad items such as lettuce, tomatoes, onions cucumber, carrots, etc. as well as pilaf and white rice. The dessert options weren't nothing special, just diced pineapple and rice pudding. At 2:30 pm, when the buffet closed, I asked for more tandoori chicken, and the manager gently brought me some extra pieces. A really nice gesture.
We paid $9.95 + tax, which is a good deal comparing to most of Indian buffets.<//text>< UserId.>

<Review>We decided to try the FH last night as we were both wanting burger type fare on a Friday night and as close as this place is to our house we had never been there. Walking up to the door there was a lively crowd in the patio at the front. Entering the establishment it impressed as being roomy with the bar and dining areas at opposite sides. The waiting staff was friendly. My wife ordered the tri-tip sandwich and I ordered the blue cheese, bacon burger, medium. The tri-tip was tasty, but tough. Similarly my burger was tasty, but dry.  When it arrived I wondered how I was going to take a bite from a 5" thick sandwich. My onion rings we good and my wife's fries were crispy. The mid rating is due to the high cost - at least $3 higher per sandwich than anywhere  else we've been in Fresno, and the lackluster punch of the food. Sawleaf in the marketplace completely solves my withdrawals for delicious Vietnamese food when I'm in Irvine :)

The location is very modern, clean, and super cute inside! They have really cool artwork and I love the layout of the store because it feels so open and bright all the time!

The service is amazing- everyone is really friendly and they always check up on their tables even though it's not a full service restaurant. Calvin, the owner, is seriously so passionate about the food and that shows through the quality and consistency. He really cares about his customers and that definitely translates to his staff as well.

I feel like I've tried most of the menu by now so I'll break it down:

Beef pho: the broth is amazing! It's super hearty and you honestly don't need any sauces because it's so flavorful on its own
I really appreciate the fact that there are separate broths for the beef, chicken, and vegetarian
The soy garlic tofu pho is also surprisingly Delicious even though I loveeeee meat

Spring rolls: so light and refreshing~ I also love the dipping sauce and it's great with sriracha

Egg roll bites: perfectly crispy and a great appetizer since they're so small and there's a lot a lot so it's easy to share

Banh mi: I love how the bread here is perfectly toasted so it's crunchy but also soft! It doesn't hurt your gums like some of the other banh mi places :) I've trade the lemongrass beef, chicken, and pork belly and they are all so good so I'd recommend Any of them!

Bun (vermicelli) and salad: this is my go to when I want something healthier feeling especially cause there's so many greens~

Loaded sweet potato fries: I prefer these with the shrimp :) it's another good appetizer and the sriracha aioli is bomb like always~

Sparkling mint limeade: my favorite drink here because it's super refreshing and light!

Vietnamese coffee: really creamy and smooth :) it's also sweet and strong just as it should be~

All in all, I love everything here and I'd recommend sawleaf to anyone because they have such a huge variety</Text>

<Review>Casual pho, but not for the experienced pho eater.

I was excited that a new Vietnamese food place popped up in Irvine. Came to check out the Pho since my previous favorite pho place (Thuan Kieu) left Irvine.  I was immediately disappointed by the lack of choices on the menu. 3 kinds of pho, 3 kinds of banh mi, 1 bun....  Ok, I get it, it's not a Vietnamese restaurant at all; it's a cafe....  But choices are more limited than a food truck!

I ordered the Pho supreme. The brisket were in pieces, broken mostly.  The tai was all clumped together indicating that it was cooked in a strainer. I would have preferred my tai be laid out and cooked in the bowl by the hot broth.

The noodles were also packed too tightly, but cooked well. Broth is a bit light for my tastes (some may call it watery) and definitely not hot enough.

True to its name, they serve the culantro herb ("saw leaf") with the Pho. It's is a must have for a good pho experience üòâ.<//Review><Pics>None</Pics>< resp>
None</resp>

<user_name>Mark Sanders (Adeco Landscaping)< /user_name><Time>1518052841053</Time><Rate>1<//Rate>< Review>
Scammers!!!!!!!
Review written on 19/02/201

SCROLL DOWN PAST REVIEWS AS THIS COMPANY HAS TRIED TO COVER UP THE TRUE NEGATIVE REVIEWS!!!!!!!!!

See Scamadvisor website
See Rip off report website
Also may be linked to gettingfrontpage website
Also see complaintsboard forum

Getvisibleweb ripped me off!! Almost $1,000 Australian Dollars. I am a landscape gardener and earn less than $40,000 AU per year before tax. They were extremely misleading from the beginning to the end. I am still in the process of trying to remove the website they created.
Just to name a few mistakes they made-

1.) When first contacted by Getvisibleweb, I was quoted a price and a for the initial website and also the SEO settings to gain first page positioning on google. They then tried to change/ increase the prices thinking that I would not notice.
2.) I was told initially that within 3-4 weeks my business would be on the first page of google. Then after the 4 weeks they said it would take 8 weeks, and this continued.
3.) I was asked to answer a list of business details that they would use for the website and SEO settings which I answered all in writing (email typed document) that also included the keyword settings that I knew prospective clients would type to find business's such as mine however, I received a phone call about 3-4 weeks later asking for the same details that they had already received, They told me there was a technical error and the information was lost.
3.) I specifically asked them to only use information and photo's from my previous free wix website as I knew what important information clients here in my region of Australia need to know however, they created a website full of misleading information that was not even relevant to my business including a photo of a guy hosing his roof with a normal garden hose which was suppose to indicate that I provide a pressure-cleaning service. Too many content mistakes to mention, the list goes on.
4.) In the document that I emailed including my business details, I had specified to not list my home address as I provide a mobile service only. My home address was on the website for months after I told them of this mistake. After each mistake, I was told 'We are very sorry and it will never happen again'. It kept happening. During our phone communication almost every time they asked me for information that I had already supplied them with in regards to my website preferences.
6.) How I think they really fooled me was that after almost 3 months of signing up they sent me a report of the keyword settings and the page my business was listed in on google. One set of two keyword was successful in getting my business to the 1st page however, it was not a keyword that any client would type to search for the services I provide. It was not one of the keywords I had specified in writing and it was obvious that the only reason my business was on the first page of google was because no-one else in their right mind would actually type these words in to look for business's such as mine.

This was when I decided to pull the plug as it was obvious Getvisible was not, and still is not providing a genuine service. I have asked repeatedly for a refund however, they told me that they have completed everything they said they would. How do people like this sleep at night? So upsetting and it has been stressful and damaging to my business! I have since done research and have read other stories in forums including one very unhappy customer explaining that this is a fraudulent company- which you can find at complaintsboard forum

Update: I posted the above review yesterday and just received a phone call from Getvisibleweb today:
Getvisible web called me today offering me a 50% refund if I take down this review.

I refused!!!!

I am now in the process of asking other business's who have used Getvisibleweb to tell their story. If you have been ripped-off by Getvisibleweb and have a similar experience to mine, please write you're review on this site. If we all make a stand, we can stop this from happening to others!!!!< /Review>

I think my time here was dampened by two  things:
1. The majority of the seating is on high chairs.  I hate high chairs. I'm super short and these have always been uncomfortable for me.
2. The table right next to us included two families where the adults didn't give AF about what the kids were doing.  One of the kids would pick up a fry and throw it on the ground.  Would grab a handful of noodles an throw them on the ground.  By the time they left the entire ground and that side of the table were covered in food.  Not cool people.

< Text>
It is really hard to do everything well but this place does it... They have excellent brunch and dinner food, cocktails, beer selection, food for a wide variety of appetizers (oysters to mac n cheese to charcuterie plate) for all sorts of tastes, outdoor seating, and even TVs for those who wanna keep tabs on the game. It's a great place for first dates. The ambiance is lively but the light is dim and the setting is cozy. I have been here at least 4 times. They also have an excellent selection for brunch and your choice of bottomless mimosas or sangria. They have a pizza with a cracked egg, excellent choice of appetizers. Service has been hit or miss. The hosts always seem to be on it but the waiters are not reliably excellent. I doesn't change my opinion. This place rocks. A staple for any event or just an escape if you are in the SF valley.  Happy hour is Sunday thru Thursday and I think it's 4pm - 6pm. I can't wait to go back.<//Text>

<rate>3</rate>< Review>
This place is usually on point but the service took a nose dive this last time.

After getting seated it took 10 minutes before the server came over and greeted us. I guess the benefit of that was that we had more than enough time to read the menu but no way in hell we were going to order anything beyond dinner for fear of not knowing when we would ever see our server again.

It took about 30-40 minutes for the food to arrive which is pretty excessive for some burgers in my opinion. Five minutes after our food arrived the server came to check on us but at this point, we didn't need her help because we decided to go walk up to the host and bussers to ask them for additional items like red pepper flakes and extra ketchup.

Fortunately, the food was good but seeing your server twice over 50-60 minutes is simply horrible service.

I'll go back because I am local, but it will be long time before I do.</Review>

< Pictures>

<Rating>5<//Rating><text>Food and drinks here are great. Never knew about this place. I will definitely go back.< /text><response>None< /response><GmapID>0x80c297c57824dfff:0x905f216b3f315606<//GmapID>< user>
101214766747337496297</user>
</record></dataset><record>
<Gmap_id>0x80c297c57824dfff:0x905f216b3f315606< /Gmap_id>< Review>
My friend and I kept passing by On The Thirty and finally decided to give it a try. We came in on a Tuesday night, so it wasn't too busy. There were a good amount of people seated outside on the patio but we were seated inside quick enough.

The bar is the length of the room and all of the tables are high tops with very comfortable seating, perfect to sink into after having a few drinks  We ordered from the mixology menu a On the mojito, blackberry smash, and I had the pina picante (pictured). Everybody was very satisfied with their drinks and they were quite strong, enough that my friend had to swap her drink with our other friend. The pina picante has the perfect amount of heat, and I love anything quite spicy.

For food, my friends had the bacon-wrapped dates (A according to them but there's only four and they're small, so pricey in the end), the Montreal poutine (again A - the portion was plenty and the cheese curds melt perfectly), and the mac and cheese, which looked and apparently was delectable but again small and seemed pricey for the amount (though they do use local ingredients as much as possible!). I just went with the truffle fries, which seemed mediocre but the chipotle dipping sauce made up for that.

I would come back for the drinks - the beer menu looked amazing as well - but pass on the appetizers/food unless I'm celebrating a special occasion.< /Review>

<Text>I can appreciate the effort of On the Thirty and also the selection of strictly California craft beer on tap.

This definitely has a wine and upscale sports bar feel to it rather than a gastropub. The vibe here is definitely not trendy and caters to an older Valley crowd.

The hosts outside were not too friendly during my second visit. We wanted to sit at a table and they said "oh, that's for groups of four."  Later on, I saw a couple sit at that table.

The food selection or how the food is presented on the menu is not too exciting to me.  It feels overpriced for what it is.

I personally prefer the gastropub vibe at Local Peasant over On the Thirty. The staff seem to be more passionate, better trained, professional, and knowledgeable.<//Text><pictures>None< /pictures>< resp>
